# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Firefox CSS Style Resolution to Layout Paint Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the style change notification, the frame style recomputation, the dirty-frame reflow scheduling, the display list construction, and the WebRender layer update.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

76-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced the complete CSS style change to layout paint chain in Mozilla Firefox/Gecko. Here's a summary of what I found:

## The CSS Style Change to Paint Chain

The chain consists of 5 major stages:

### 1. **Style Change Notification** 
- `layout/style/RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()` - Posts the restyle event when a style changes

### 2. **Frame Style Recomputation**
- `layout/style/ServoStyleSet::ResolveStyle()` - Resolves styles using the Servo CSS engine
- `servo/ports/geckolib/glue.rs::Servo_ResolveStyle()` - Rust FFI binding to Servo

### 3. **Dirty Frame Reflow Scheduling**
- `layout/style/RestyleManager::StyleChangeReflow()` - Interprets change hints
- `layout/base/PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()` - Marks frames dirty and schedules reflow

### 4. **Display List Construction**
- `layout/generic/nsIFrame::BuildDisplayListForStackingContext()` - Builds display items
- `layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder::AttemptPartialUpdate()` - Optimizes by only rebuilding changed portions
- `layout/painting/nsDisplayList` - Manages the display item list

### 5. **WebRender Layer Update**
- `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager::EndTransactionWithoutLayer()` - Processes display list
- `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeChild::EndTransaction()` - Sends to GPU process via IPC

`servo/ports/geckolib/glue.rs`.\\n\\n2. **Dirty Tracking**: Gecko uses a sophisticated dirty frame tracking system with multiple state bits (NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY, NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN) to optimize reflow.\\n\\n3. **Retained Display Lists**: Rather than rebuilding the entire display list every frame, Firefox tracks which frames changed and only rebuilds affected portions, then merges them with retained items.\\n\\n4. **IPC Boundary**: WebRender communication happens through `WebRenderBridgeChild`, which serializes display list data and sends it to a separate GPU process for rendering.\\n\\n5. **Change Hints System**: The `nsChangeHint` enumeration (in `layout/style/nsChangeHint.h`) encodes what layout work is needed based on style differences, guiding the reflow reflow.\\n\\n3. **Retained Display Lists**: Rather than rebuilding the entire display list every frame, Firefox tracks which frames changed and only rebuilds affected portions, then merges them with retained items.\\n\\n4. **IPC Boundary**: WebRender communication happens through `WebRenderBridgeChild`, which serializes display list data and sends it to a separate GPU process for
